Dao Equaling the Heavens
============================================================

76: Chapter 68: A Snap Conceals the Sky

76 -68: A Snap Conceals the Sky

Gu Wen leapt across rooftops, heading swiftly toward the south gate to escape Bianjing.

A figure was rapidly closing in from behind.

Glancing back and recognizing it was Hee Huan, he chose not to turn and counterattack.

As the pursuer drew near, their gaze was complex, filled with many doubts and words to say, but knowing the urgency of the moment, said, “Brother Hongchen, once out of the city, it’s best to take the water path.

Otherwise, if you encounter the army led by Wenren Wu, it will be a hopeless situation.”

“Why?” Gu Wen countered, “Armies move slowly, and can hardly form an encirclement for a killing blow.

I might fear him alone, but leading a group, can they even fly?”

“Military might…

he’s the third-ranked general from the Mixed Element Sect, merging array and military dharma forms.

His Qianyuan Secret Skill can conjure thousands of Fake Spirit Images as soldiers and dharma forms as generals, an army in one man.”

Hee Huan was not one to beat around the bush, and he knew there was no time to waste.

The True Monarch from the military sect who had just entered the city had noticed them and was swiftly closing in.

“Do you see that gigantic dharma form?

That’s not its actual size.

It’s the Fake Spirit Images combining with the dharma form to manifest the army’s might.

The downside is they can’t hide and their feet must touch the ground.

It’s a flaw, like an array that traps you in by drawing a boundary with a gate of life.”

Military might was an extremely formidable concept, virtually a mobile array, combining the power of an array with mobility.

But nothing in the world is perfect; when something is extraordinarily strong in one aspect, it inevitably has flaws.

“Take care of yourself, I can’t help you anymore.”

With that, Hee Huan immediately turned to flee.

Although he had always wanted to owe Gu Wen a favor, under these circumstances, even he couldn’t hold out.

Simply providing some intelligence was already going above and beyond; he, Hee Huan, had done right by the name of a friend.

“Thank you.”

Gu Wen changed direction, heading for a water gate near the south gate, used for boats to transport goods into Bianjing.

Even though the boat he arranged may have already departed at this time, it couldn’t have gone far.

He could certainly catch up using a smaller boat.

Looking down at the green pearl hanging around his neck, the Jade-eyed Water Wave Pearl had the ability to repel water.

As long as his mana was plentiful, he could stay underwater for a day without issues.

Whoosh!

Feeling a chill on his back, Gu Wen whirled around and thrust his spear, colliding with another mana-infused golden spear flying toward him.

The gold spear couldn’t match the hardness of Gu Wen’s heavy spear and shattered upon impact.

From afar, a colossal figure drew its bowstring, shooting another arrow.

Boom!

Gu Wen shattered it into gold dust with his spear.

Yet a relentless stream of golden arrows rained down, slowing him with each step.

Five miles away from the South Water Gate, ships were visible in the distance, but the dharma form soldiers had already blocked Gu Wen’s path.

Below, a general clad in tiger-faced armor and wielding a large halberd stood three zhang tall, bold and imposing.

“The Saint Emperor decrees, surrender and you may live.”

“Further talk is pointless.”

Gu Wen rocketed forward like a shot arrow, unleashing a full-powered thrust with a flood dragon’s ferocity.

Wenren Wu faced the onslaught head-on, undaunted by Flame Dharma’s killing aura, and unfazed by Gu Wen’s immense strength.

Their collision sent shockwaves through the air, roofing tiles whistling in the wind while the people inside the houses trembled from fear.

The city of Bianjing had not emptied; the reason the streets were deserted was that people knew to hide from trouble.

Whether it was immortals brawling, a civil uprising, or a coup, most people would stay out of sight.

Boom!

Suddenly, a deafening clash of metal, like bursting firecrackers, filled the air around the South Water Gate.

Gu Wen and Wenren Wu exchanged dozens of blows in a flash, their arms and weapons blurring into a dense, impenetrable flurry.

This time, though, Gu Wen was on the losing end; with each clashing strike, his palms split open and blood began to seep out.

Clearly, his opponent had held back, intending to capture Gu Wen alive.

The Third Level of Dao Foundation and military dharma forms could not rival a True Monarch.

Realizing the enemy wanted to take him alive, Gu Wen’s strength in his hands grew weaker as if nearing exhaustion.

To turn weakness into victory when facing a stronger opponent, one had to wait for the opponent to expose a flaw and then strike with all their might in one fatal blow.

If that failed, there was no other option but to escape.

In his plans, he had not anticipated a True Monarch’s interference, nor did he expect Wenren Wu to return from thousands of miles away in just a matter of days.

Wenren Wu also slowed down his attack, but in that instant, Gu Wen’s eyes contained myriad deadly lights, as he used up all his mana, with the Flame Dharma form coiling around him, and the Five Spirit Forms appeared.

A spear thrust out, a streak of crimson light condensed to the extreme emerged.

The Flame Spear possessed a hint of divine skills, and it was the only move designed to kill.

The Soldier Dharma Form could not withstand it, and a halberd, which seemed like a Spiritual Treasure, was knocked aside, as the crimson light attached to the spear tip was about to touch the neck, and a strand of hair just slightly stirred by the wind turned to ash gray.

One chi, one cun, one hair…

In a flash, a hundred zhang of golden light rose, and limitless martial spirits arrived, pulling Gu Wen into the domain of the dharma form.

A towering Divine General stood above the battlefield, with thousands of Spirit Form soldiers arranged in military formation.

Eighth Level of Dao Foundation, three of which were fulfilled.

The Dark Heavy Spear had no possibility of advancing further, as the martial spirits themselves formed an array, founded on soldiers, with generals forming the array, an array that could be established in an instant.

Wenren Wu’s position was always at the heart of the array; he had the strength of ten thousand jun, yet also the finesse of diverting a thousand pounds with four liang; between the spear tip and the throat, the martial spirit turned into thousands of blades and shields.

The Dark Heavy Spear broke one chi of its tip, Gu Wen flew backward, landing as he had anticipated by the river bank, crashing through the dragon bone of an official ship, yet he seemed to have no strength to flee.

A mouthful of fresh blood spat out, the knock to the head together with the assault on his Divine Soul nearly made Gu Wen pass out.

‘He’s tens of times stronger than that old eunuch.’

He finally sensed the specific level of the opponent’s cultivation, the Eighth Level of Dao Foundation with three levels fulfilled, so at this stage, he basically had no chance of winning.

In the distance, a drop of blood flowed from Wenren Wen’s throat, he reached up to wipe it off, then looked at the blood on his fingertip somewhat dumbfounded.

Could he actually trade wounds with me?

Gu Wen was only at the Foundation Establishment Third Level, and he was at the Eighth Level; moreover, he also had the foundation of a True Monarch.

There should be no chance they would be a match, not even a chance to resist.

The gap and bridging the gap, these are the best standards to measure a person’s talent.

If I were a step later in returning to Bianjing, then no one could stop him.

“Gu Wen, your talent is enough for me to exert my full strength.

This is your last chance, become the Crown Prince of Daqian or die here.”

Wenren Wu stepped toward Gu Wen, lying inside the cabin, his vague understanding of why the Saint Emperor valued Gu Wen so much—the opponent’s talent would surely surpass his own given time.

Five years of servitude and still, he managed to establish three levels of foundation, and with just those, he could injure my skin and flesh.

And if I don’t accept being a dog now, in the future it is I who will die and my Dao will be destroyed.

Gu Wen struggled to get up, wiping the fresh blood from the corner of his mouth, and said, “But I haven’t used my full strength yet.”

“Oh?” Wenren Wu was interested; he stopped in his tracks and, with great dignity, said, “It’s not honorable for me to bully the weak, so if you have any moves left, feel free to use them; I won’t stop you.”

Gu Wen swallowed the pill Yu Hua had given him, a warm flow soothing his pain, then he stood up and walked toward the break in the cabin he had created—his palm glowed with a faint light, and two characters faintly emerged.

“Qingcang.”

These characters had already reacted when he faced Wenren Wu.

If it hadn’t been for the unexpected event of Wenren Wu, naturally, he could have run, but now, with a True Monarch in pursuit, if he didn’t shake things up, it would be his problem.

Gu Wen softly said, “I ask the immortal to aid me.”

Background is also a kind of strength; you’ve been pressuring me with your background for so long, can’t I press back on you?

Wenren Wu felt a chill shoot straight to his forehead, and without a moment’s hesitation, he charged at Gu Wen with all his might.

Boom!

A sudden tumult rose like a thousand layers of waves.

Above the Nine Heavens, a thousand miles away, a snap of the fingers covered the sky.

A faint profound sound descended from heaven.

“I will naturally help you.”

============================================================
Dao Equaling the Heavens
============================================================

77: Chapter 69: The Power of the Nine Level Fulfilled Dao Foundation

77 -69: The Power of the Nine Level Fulfilled Dao Foundation

The clouds collapsed, leaving a clear sky for miles, as a finger descended from the heavens.

Gu Wen looked up, as if the entire world had paused, with the wind-whipped dead leaves suspended mid-air, and the hundred-yard-tall golden figure raising its shield toward the Heavenly True Immortal’s mighty light.

His Dao Foundation was similar to Yu Hua’s, both originating from the same source.

Although their power differed as dirt from clouds, he could still feel the gap, even clearer than his awareness of Wenren Wu.

It was a mountain reaching into the heavens, a giant tens of thousands of yards tall.

I saw her as a mayfly, soaring across the cosmos and glimpsing the great sun.

Yu Hua’s strength, all nine levels of her Dao Foundation were fulfilled.

Boom!

The sky’s finger fell, and in an instant, the dharma form soldiers kneeled, making the whole of Bianjing tremble.

On either side of Bianjing, a wide avenue of ten yards collapsed, countless blue stone slabs shattered into rubble.

Wenren Wu knelt on the ground, using all his strength to support himself with his hands, his tiger’s mouth spewing blood, his body’s flesh and muscles exceeded their limits and thus burst.

The power of the Eighth Level Dao Foundation, the ability of the Third Level fulfilled, the method of ten thousand soldiers.

He exhausted every tactic and ounce of strength, fighting for a slim chance of survival.

“Ah!!!!”

A half-step stance, lifting heaven with a raise!

The golden figure supported heaven’s finger, with the cultivation of the Eighth Level Dao Foundation, it contested the Taoist Heavenly Girl for a moment – such talent was indeed rare.

Immortal Land housed no mediocre individuals; Wenren Wu was able to suppress the national fate for ten years on the frontier, contending against northern invaders and facing both covert and overt attacks from various True Monarchs.

He was among the top warriors of his era.

If it were outside, he could dominate an area easily, but unfortunately, this was Immortal Land.

The sky’s finger pressed down again, the soldiers’ dharma forms shattered like frost, breaking inch by inch.

Hum!

A deep dragon’s chant came, a streak of golden light enveloping Wenren Wu and moving him half a yard at a critical moment, dodging the sky’s finger.

The sky’s finger touched the ground silently, barely stirring a wisp of dust.

The sky tilted like a mountain collapsing, but the retraction was gentle like the wind.

Wenren Wu, looking at his empty right arm, managed a carefree smile after the disaster.

“I, too, have contested against celestial might for a moment, magnificent!”

From a distance, Gu Wen came holding a broken spear, dust slowly settling, and Wenren Wu, dragging his battered body, rose and with a halberd in his left hand, slowly walked towards Gu Wen.

Gu Wen advised, “General, as long as the green hills are there, one need not worry about firewood.”

Though he approached, it was because the opposing Aura still locked onto him, stubbornly not letting go.

“If you run away, I’ll be mere firewood.

But this time, I only outmatch your True Monarch’s foundation, yet with your talent, you should have a ten percent chance of winning.”

Wenren Wu introspected, his Mana nine parts gone, his right arm severed, his dharma form damaged.

His face fierce as a tiger, as if his aura devoured thousands of miles, he loudly declared, “I am the Hundred Battle True Monarch, disciple of the Third Mixed Element Sect, once ranked third on the Human List and eighth on the Earth List!

Young man, state your sect; I do not kill the nameless.”

“Gu Wen, apprentice of the methods of Upper Pure, without sect or school, ranked tenth on the Human List and fifth on the Earth List.”

Gu Wen’s voice was calm, conserving his strength amidst life and death combat.

Around them, people from various factions gathered again.

Some stood on the distant city walls looking down, others stood on rooftops a few miles away, with those bold and skilled directly observing from within a hundred yards.

Lu Chan gracefully landed on the rooftop, her snow-white skin striking against the black tiles, just as a handsome, pale-faced young master landed nearby.

“Young Master Hee of the ninth rank?”

The handsome young master nodded slightly and said, “I’ve seen the Fox Fairy.”

Though they were strangers, the battle below had already begun.

Old and new talents of the heavens clashed for the first time, with newcomers challenging the seasoned True Monarchs.

Bang!

Gu Wen and Wenren Wu moved faster than the wild wind, swift as the wind, clashing like thunder.

Not at a disadvantage?!

The young talents looked on in astonishment; they were just beginning to understand how strong Gu Wen was, ranking among the top talents

of his generation.

But even with high talent, there should be limits.

After all, his opponent was a True Monarch, a combat-savvy Military True Monarch.

Lu Chan’s eyes shone.

Unskilled in close combat, she turned to ask, “Young Master Hee, how would you fare against a True Monarch?”

Young Master Hee didn’t answer at first, gestured for payment, and then, taking a Pill, finally replied, “Against hum, I wouldn’t last ten moves.

The Hundred Battle True Monarch uses his body as formation, can reverse any situation, and the military method is intrinsically suited for close combat.

Additionally, as a Body Refinement practitioner, I cannot compensate for my shortcomings.”

“And Gu Wen?”

“He would die; his spear technique is purely lethal.”

“So Gu Wen surpasses the True Monarch?”

Lu Chan’s eyes sparkled; she saw in him the shadow of another, the Tao Child of the Sanqing Taoist Sect.

Young Master Hee shook his head, “Gu Wen is not yet a match for the True Monarch, still at a disadvantage, but my True Monarch knows the Hundred Battle True Monarch, and I don’t know Gu Wen.

The Fox Fairy should know, the shod fear the barefoot, and if he challenged me, I would definitely concede.”

“….”

Lu Chan was speechless; she understood the importance of background, but Young Master Hee had an aloof face for nothing.

Boom!

For the first time, the two combatants below separated from their entangled fight and then collided like two fiery meteors, exerting all their strength.

Spear against halberd, warrior against general, they displayed the utmost skill of long weapons.

Above them, a divine finger descended again, as a yellow dragon soared to meet the sky.

—————–

Yu Hua rode the White Dragon Horse at high speed through the sky.

Flight in the Immortal Land was challenging; the horse’s hooves continuously bled, and occasionally, rays of golden light shot toward them from a distance.

This was already a battle at the level of the Third Realm outside, yet it was taking place in the Immortal Land.

It was madness, sheer madness!

Old Donkey couldn’t imagine how powerful the Lord Emperor was outside.

He himself was a True Monarch, but the other’s strength was so great that he could barely comprehend it.

He couldn’t even begin to imagine Yu Hua’s power or the depth of the Immortal’s power within her.

The difference between the Four Realms was like that between mud and clouds; the levels above the Four Realms were like chasms in the heavens, immeasurable.

The distinctions between realms were divided into ranks of three, six, and nine, with immortals and mortals not even on the same level.

Mud piled into a mountain could not turn into clouds.

“Yu Hua, you and I should not be enemies,”

said the voice of the Lord Emperor.

Yu Hua responded bluntly, “I just need to take him with me.”

“That’s not in accordance with the agreement.

He must stay in Bianjing and become the Crown Prince of Daqian,”

the Lord Emperor retorted, not only because of Gu Wen’s talent but also because he needed a lever to balance the Taoist Heavenly Girl.

If the Guardian’s identity was not in his own hands, then he would have nothing to do with the Immortality Pill.

With no benefits to gain, he would also leave behind a major risk.

“I shall treat him as my own, imparting all my knowledge.

Once this period in the Immortal Land is over, he will naturally be free.”

“Get lost!”

Yu Hua’s voice inevitably carried a hint of murderous intent, this having touched her sore spot.

This was the uncut jade she had discovered and nurtured.

She believed that Gu Wen would inevitably retrace the path of her mentor and surpass all contemporary True Monarchs.

The Lord Emperor apparently saw some hints of this and thus wanted to pick the fruits of her labor.

But Yu Hua had witnessed Gu Wen’s growth firsthand.

Without seeing it with her own eyes, she couldn’t have imagined someone advancing to the third level of Dao foundation in just half a year.

Anyone who tries to take him from her would die!

“Yu Hua, I only want to pass on my legacy to him to neutralize the karma; I don’t have to take him as my disciple.”

“Get lost!”

“Yu Hua, why go to such lengths?”

The Lord Emperor’s voice sounded a bit dejected; he understood that a young person might be eager, so there was no point in being upset with him.

By forcefully keeping the other party here and continuously offering affection, he could gradually tame him.

But why was Yu Hua as furious as Gu Wen?

He had already compromised, almost to the point of saying, “Give me a chance to make it right.”

Even Old Donkey thought it was a bit much.

The Lord Emperor was no ordinary person, and the request he made had no downside for them.

But he was slightly different from other True Monarchs.

As a gatekeeper of the Sanqing Taoist Sect, what he saw most every year was a bunch of young people deeply in love.

Once emotions were involved, people became unreasonable.

And at this time, it wasn’t about right or wrong; it was about choosing sides.

Why would the Three Pure Ones’ Divine Beast side with Yu Hua and help the Lord Emperor if not insane?

Old Donkey communicated telepathically: “Leave right or wrong for later, Little Ancestor, but remember one thing—if offended, kill without leaving any chance!”

“Understood.”

Yu Hua nodded.

Suddenly, a beam of white light shot straight into the sky from the direction of Bianjing, piercing the barriers of the Immortal Land.

—————–

In the palace, the Pill Furnace blazed fiercely.

For ten years now, the Lord Emperor had continuously thrown Spiritual Medicine into it.

A thousand years ago, he had learned of the existence of the Immortality Pill.

Therefore, to devise plans for obtaining the Immortality Pill, he sold off his doctrine, exhausted the affection of relatives and friends, and established Daqian in the Immortal Land.

The presence of the Heavenly Girl from the Three Pure Ones, which implied the power of an Immortal, was the first upheaval.

Gu family’s only son, hidden for five years, reaching the third level of Dao foundation, was the second upheaval.

“The world is impermanent, but the result remains the same.”

Two Imperial Decree wooden plaques lay in front of the Lord Emperor, one white and one black.

The white could carry messages out of the Immortal Land, directly to Sanqing Taoist Sect headquarters, costing the value of thousands of medicine fruits.

The black could resound through heaven and earth, piercing through the Nine Netherworld and Nine Heavens, from the Human Race’s Earth Realm to the Jianmu monster sea, from the netherworld to beyond the skies, valued at half a Taoist Soldier.

The Lord Emperor’s greatest leverage in dealing with the Sanqing Taoist Sect wasn’t the Guardian’s token, but the two wooden plaques in front of him.

He picked up the white Imperial Decree and waved it out of the Immortal Land.

The Daoist Sect would help him block the Taoist Heavenly Girl.

If that failed, he would call for the True Monarchs worldwide to join forces.

The name he bore in the past struck awe across the world, almost suffocating all beings.

When the three great holy lands of the Daoist Sect—Yuqing, Shangqing, and Taiqing—united, the Four Land Buddhist Sect of the Buddhist Sect and the Nine Abysses, Eighteen Caves of the Demon Sect were reduced to just Four Abysses and Eight Caves, and their Jianmu monster sea of 108 Grotto Heavens was reduced to just 36 Grotto Heavens.

His survival in the current era meant for contemporary strong beings, it was as if the great Dao were about to break.

============================================================
Dao Equaling the Heavens
============================================================

78: Chapter 70: The Grandmaster of Taiqing Descends, Escape to Survival

78 -70: The Grandmaster of Taiqing Descends, Escape to Survival

Yu Hua was a hundred miles from Bianjing when a clear light descended from the sky, and the figure of a Daoist, ethereal as white jade, appeared, his aura like a white cloud.

Sanqing Taoist Sect, Taiqing Sect leader, Yun Miao Venerable.

Yun Miao Venerable spoke in an even tone,

“Fellow Daoist Ao, please stop, and Heavenly Girl, listen to my words.”

A mass of white clouds enveloped the two, and the old donkey couldn’t penetrate even slightly, and of course, he didn’t think of breaking the opponent’s Daoist Skill.

This was the leader of the Taiqing Sect, and although he wasn’t the current Venerable, there was no guarantee that within the next millennium, he wouldn’t be the one to take over as Venerable.

Yu Hua coldly said, “Is Uncle Master Yun Miao trying to stop me?”

“I am no Huayang, who I have already stopped, but I won’t stop you.

Since the Heavenly Girl has grown her wings, she can naturally speak to the Daoist Sect about her direction, and there are some things that you should also know.”

Yun Miao Venerable waved his sleeve to dissipate the cloud and mist.

He had no intention of intervening in the matter of becoming an Immortal, but he suddenly felt a great catastrophe approaching and couldn’t help but come to see what this Heavenly Girl of his own family was planning to do.

“A thousand years ago, the theft of the Scripture Pavilion in the Daoist Sect led to the upheaval we see today in Daqian.

It wasn’t because the Daoist Sect changed the Guardian for profit, but because by the time the Daoist Sect was aware, the Gu family was already gone, and the Lord Emperor had information about the Immortality Pill.”

Yu Hua retorted, “The Daoist Sect has fifteen True Monarchs, are they afraid of him alone?”

“I am better than him by a bit, and naturally, the Daoist Sect won’t be afraid of him either.”

Yun Miao Venerable continued, his tone unfluctuating,

“It’s just that the Daoist Sect and he reached an agreement to seek the Immortality Pill and give him a slice of its root.

The price is that he will take over the powers of the Guardian, and the two of you together can handle any sect’s blockade with ease.

Without him, if you become enemies with him, the sect can only help you hold off a few old monsters.”

“Why, then, would the Daoist Sect, for a mere mortal, expose the Immortality Pill and push the revival of Qingcang Master towards no hope?”

Yu Hua said, “Gu Wen is already at the Third Level of Dao Foundation, and possesses a dharma form of the military way.”

“He indeed has the demeanor of a Daoist child, and the Daoist Sect will naturally protect his life, only, it would not be worth it to break with the Lord Emperor.”

Yun Miao Venerable slightly shook his head as he was aware of Gu Wen’s talents, as well as the demands of the Lord Emperor.

This wasn’t a single choice issue; the Lord Emperor didn’t want Gu Wen’s life, just that Gu Wen stayed in Bianjing.

Yu Hua’s voice turned slightly cold, “So, does the Daoist Sect mean to make him suffer once more?”

“For the greater good, the Daoist Sect and Daqian will compensate him.”

Yun Miao Venerable said something that Yu Hua found extremely discomforting.

She had thought the same half a year ago; did they now want her to make the same mistake again?

“Unless you have other reasons, why would the Daoist Sect indulge him?

I won’t stop you, but can you stop all the True Monarchs of the world?”

Yu Hua’s gaze sank slightly, thousand of Divine Thoughts swirling, unable to make a decision immediately.

Should she expose Gu Wen’s talents?

Would revealing his talents make the situation even worse?

At this moment, everyone knew Gu Wen had achieved the Third Level of Dao Foundation, but believed he cultivated the Cultivation Technique left by the Gu family, which meant he had achieved the Third Level of Dao Foundation in five years, making him a top genius.

But only she knew, Gu Wen had cultivated only half a year to reach the Third Level of Dao Foundation, and had also understood from the Xuanming Spear his own dharma form.

She hadn’t given him any insights into the military way, yet Gu Wen forcibly stepped out his own military dharma form.

Thus, no reason was needed, nor needed to be explained.

Yu Hua slightly lifted her head, and the third eye on her brow shone radiantly, the surrounding white clouds shattering inch by inch.

“I indulge him, and that is sufficient.”

Yun Miao Venerable paused briefly, then lightly smiled, “Well said, great power, the utmost that can be achieved.”

He stepped aside and no longer obstructed.

Yu Hua knew what she was doing, and was ready to bear the consequences.

She was no longer just a disciple of the sect, and had the entitlement to make decisions; the Daoist Sect cultivated disciples, not slaves.

What is the purpose of cultivation?

It is to seek a portion of carefree life.

As for the grand plans of the sect, the Daoist Sect was not yet at a stage where it had to rely on so-called grand plans to survive.

At least, Yun Miao Venerable didn’t think so; if no one became an Immortal, why shouldn’t it be he himself?

“But you have already gone against the consensus of the sect, and the Daoist Sect won’t help you anymore; whether the sect’s True Monarchs will assist you is for them to decide.”

The old donkey was flustered; he hadn’t expected things to turn out like this, and that the Daoist Sect would just give up their full support for Yu Hua so suddenly.

It was as if a state policy of the dynasty had been suddenly abolished; protecting Yu Hua was no longer an obligation.

But this was just the appearance.

With Yun Miao Venerable’s arrival, it also meant that Huayang had lost his influence.

Did it mean…

he was moving up a level?

In the Four Realms, Twelve Levels, the Fourth Realm is honored as True Monarchs, and most remained at the First Level, the Enlightenment Realm, including himself.

The other two levels were Harmonization and Attainment, which were not two sequential stages but two different branching paths.

It was the ancient dispute between Innate and Transient; Innates pursued Harmonization, Transients pursued Enlightenment.

Those who harmonized, melded with heaven and earth.

Those who attained, transcended heaven and earth.

People used to think the path of Enlightenment was stronger, transcending heaven and earth was a phrase that inherently inspired longing, and Qingcang Daoist was also a transcendent.

Later, people realized it was Qingcang who was powerful, not Enlightenment itself.

Yun Miao Venerable followed the path of Harmonization, Huayang Venerable the path of Enlightenment.

The Daoist Sect was indeed experiencing troubled times.

Yu Hua rode the dragon horse towards Bianjing, when suddenly Yun Miao Venerable called out to her, pointing in another direction.

“You’re going the wrong way.”

—————–

Bianjing.

Gu Wen and Wenren Wu each took ten steps back, both were injured, but it was only Gu Wen who was losing; it was merely a matter of how much he was losing.

Yet, the surrounding onlookers were all stunned, no one dared to call him weak.

To fight a True Monarch with only a Third Level Dao Foundation and merely be disadvantaged, this was truly an unprecedented event.

============================================================
Dao Equaling the Heavens
============================================================

79: Chapter 70: The Grandmaster of Taiqing Descends, Escape to Survival_2

79 -70: The Grandmaster of Taiqing Descends, Escape to Survival_2

Gu Wen’s form was unsteady, his body marked with countless wounds, yet the understanding of dharma form in his eyes had not dispersed and was constantly expanding.

Divine Skill one-thousandth, Divine Skill two-thousandth, Divine Skill three-thousandth…

His battles were few, and this disadvantage was unique.

Crisis signified opportunity and was also the best teacher; he had learned much from Wenren Wu.

The opponent’s techniques and various battle responses were masterful and breathtaking.

Wenren Wu, gasping for air, noticed the change in his opponent’s aura—a mix between a curse and a compliment—as he said, “You are truly a monster, to continually refine your Divine Skill while battling me.”

Dharma form nurtures Divine Skills, yet not everyone possessed Divine Skills.

Geniuses gather Spirit Form, prodigies nurture dharma form, sect heirs each master one Divine Skill.

Yet, Gu Wen was continuously understanding his own Divine Skills amidst a life and death battle.

Wenren Wu could understand advancing in Daoist Skill during combat, but he could not understand the speed of Gu Wen; it was simply too fast.

Others refined their Divine Skills over years, yet he measured it in minutes, as if he could turn every move of his opponent into nourishment.

Gu Wen glanced at the water gate behind him with the corner of his eye and spat a mouthful of blood, saying, “What use is there in understanding more when I cannot defeat the General overnight?”

At present, his Flame Spear Divine Ability was only at a thousandth, which sounded good if said it had surged threefold, but truthfully, he might not break through even after being beaten for three days and nights.

“…” Wenren Wu’s forehead veins bulged, and with a grin that was not quite a smile, he said, “Kid, I am at least an Eighth Level Dao Foundation, from the Fourth Realm.

Do you really not understand the gap between Dao Foundations?”

It wasn’t that breakthroughs during battle were useless, but that there was already a three-realm gap between the two of them.

Even if he had broken an arm and greatly damaged his strength, the disparity between them was not something that could easily be bridged.

Outside Immortal Land, Four Realms were considered, mana being the strongest, and those overcoming small realm enemies existed, yet none had overcome four realms of difference.

Within Immortal Land, Dao Foundations were considered, from First to ninth Level Dao Foundation, a fulfilled Dao Foundation might equate to two, and the rest was determined by dharma forms and Divine Skills.

In fact, Immortal Land clarified it most because many clever tactics were limited by mana; here, only Dao Foundation and reaching the peak mattered.

Wenren Wu was an Eighth Level Dao Foundation plus a third-level fulfilled Dao Foundation, which translated into the eleventh Level Heaven when converted into small realms.

Gu Wen was a third-level fulfilled Dao Foundation, converting into the sixth Level Heaven.

Dharma forms might count for one, but Wenren Wu also possessed a dharma form, so it was impossible to achieve an impact similar to the Imperial Supervisor Feng Baizhou.

Eleventh Level Heaven against Sixth Level Heaven, and that Heavenly Girl was at least at the eighteenth Level Heavens; his disparity with her was even greater than Gu Wen’s.

Ordinary foundation establishment counted as one, fulfilled counted as two.

“Back to the point, you have already lost to me twice; things happen in threes, so I ask you one last time, become Daqian’s Crown Prince, or be temporarily placed under house arrest.”

“Isn’t it death?” Gu Wen was surprised by the change in the other’s demeanor.

Wenren Wu calmly replied, “That Taoist Heavenly Girl wants to save you; thus, I cannot decide your life or death, for fear it brings about mortal peril.”

It truly was all about backing; without it, one would be completely eradicated, but with it, even deadly foes would take heed.

Gu Wen threw his battered heavy spear to the side and asked, “General, do you still have the strength?”

Wenren Wu, thinking that his opponent had given up resistance, although he had not let down his guard, still confidently responded, “Somewhat, but not as continuous as your Yuqing Daoji; my Mixed Element Dao Foundation consists in being invincible on the spot.”

“The General is quite talkative.”

“For a talented individual, I naturally enjoy conversation.”

“Then, let’s chat next time.”

“Hm?”

Plunge!

Gu Wen dove into the river, moving like a fish and quickly submerging under the water.

Wenren Wu nearly at the same time tried to stop him, Gang Qi striking the water and creating a ten-meter-high splash.

He hit Gu Wen but it was of little use.

Water is firm when met with firmness; the greater the force, the more the water is affected, thus more energy is lost.

This was his predetermined escape route.

Yu Hua once said something that Gu Wen always remembered: in Daqian, everyone becomes mundane.

No matter the level of cultivation, all need food, drink, sleep, and relief.

Consuming Pills and meditating are just other ways to meet those needs, not complete dismissals.

And he possessed a Spiritual Treasure, the Jade-eyed Water Wave Pearl, weaker in fighting but capable of controlling water.

Knowing he couldn’t win, he would surely run; now Gu Wen only regretted not being able to raid the Grand Treasury Department again.

If Wenren Wu had not come, he could have filled his Qiankun Bag!

“Indeed, he’s just like a slippery loach!”

Wenren Wu couldn’t help but curse, but he wasn’t foolish enough to chase into the water.

There is no perfect solution in the world, for if one possesses the ability to stand unbeaten, naturally, there must be a vital weakness.

He followed the river all the way to the water gate, traced Gu Wen’s aura over the city wall, and arrived outside of Bianjing, only to find not the vast plains he expected but countless chaotic residences.

Chasing all the way, he initially thought Gu Wen wouldn’t last long since Immortal Land had an ironclad rule: “All beings revert to the mundane.”

Breathing was included, which could be alleviated by water-avoidance techniques, but mana was inevitably required.

Unless he possessed a water-avoidance spiritual treasure!

Wenren Wu suddenly came to his senses and sent a divine thought toward the imperial palace, “Your majesty, please assist!”

His body was heavily injured, and he was not skilled in water combat, he really might let Gu Wen escape if he wasn’t careful.

The divine thought was sent out, but there was no response for a long time.

Suddenly, a dark light shot straight into the clouds, entering the Cultivation World.

The Daoist sound of the great path reverberated in all directions, and strands of news also reached Wenren Wu’s ears.

Qingcang, Immortality Pill, the second life…

Booming thunderously!

The earth trembled, numerous old monsters hidden had broken through their realms and arrived outside of Immortal Land.

From the Buddhist, Taoist, and Demon sects, to the Dragon Clan at the coast of the East Sea, the owners of thirty-eight Grotto Heavens from Jianmu Demon Sea swarmed over.

A Daoist in plain robes, holding a sword, ascended to the heavens and said gently, “I am Yun Miao of the Three Pure Daoist Sect, Daoist Sect of Upper Pure.

I ask you all to retreat.”

In an instant, light and shadow outside of heaven were unstable, their magical battle spanned the entire Daqian territory for a whole day and night, making it hard to distinguish day from night.

Yun Miao of Upper Pure Sect, fighting alone against several True Monarchs without falling into a disadvantage, followed by Huayang Venerable of the same sect coming forward with others, resulting in another chaotic battle.

In the end, the Sanqing Taoist Sect came out slightly superior.

Meanwhile, Yu Hua had killed two disrespectful old creatures, when she realized she had lost track of Gu Wen.

That little loach was too quick!

He didn’t need her care, he would hide by himself, and the moment she opened her eyes, she couldn’t locate him using conventional methods.

Others could not even think about it, as the range of divine thought was also restricted in Immortal Land, and currently, no one should have a broader divine thought than hers.

Sometimes, being too worry-free was not a good thing.

Yu Hua searched along the rivers, but with the vast number of tributaries in the great river, she ran herself and her old donkey breathless.

“Little ancestor, I’m afraid he can’t be found.

Let’s wait for him to appear again.”

Yu Hua was about to give up when suddenly she saw an official boat and had a thought.

“Let’s wait for him to come to us.”

—————

On the other side.

Relying on the undying nature of his Yuqing Daoji, Gu Wen swam for a day and a night, oblivious to the turmoil above.

Suddenly, he saw an official boat passing overhead.

Every month, the Grand Treasury Department sent people to collect tributes from various places, dividing the routes between land and water.

The southern water routes were well-developed and mostly relied on waterways.

Soft voices came through, visible through the water surface was the flag of the Grand Treasury Department.

“Be careful with the moving, all these are offerings to His Majesty.”

What did you say, offerings for his Daoist Highness?

Gu Wen bubbled like a water ghost, then swiftly swam upward.

============================================================
Dao Equaling the Heavens
============================================================

80: Chapter 71: The World Turns Against Us

80 -71: The World Turns Against Us

“Sanqing Daoist Sect won?”

Wenren Wu, injured and lying beside the pill furnace, could hardly believe the news he heard.

Not to mention Yun Miao, the Venerable who fought dozens of people single-handedly, could the Sanqing Daoist Sect really defeat the entire Cultivation World alone?

The Lord Emperor was applying medicine for him; with neither sorrow nor joy, he said, “The Sanqing Daoist Sect has always been unrivaled in the world, whether it’s Yun Miao, Huayang, or even some of those old timers, all have already reached the pinnacle of the Fourth Realm.”

“Moreover, they only temporarily have the upper hand; more people will come later.

If those great powers who do not entangle with the sect directly enter the Immortal Land, how many could they possibly stop?”

This was the confidence behind his deal with the sect; the Lord Emperor believed in the weight of the name Qingcang.

Those who have entered once generally wouldn’t think of entering this cursed place a second time.

The fact that Wenren Wu could fight a junior showed his mettle, and it would be no surprise if one of the top talents on the Three Rankings died on the spot.

True Monarchs are not to be trifled with outside, and inside it’s not unheard of for chaos to kill a master with wild punches.

They were all great powers who had made their names and reigned for a thousand years; most of them were very cautious with their lives.

Moreover, realms that were unattainable in the past would yield the same results if tried again; the benefits were not worth the risks.

However, Qingcang could draw out many old timers, remnants of the great war of that time.

“However, the one who is coming is Yun Miao, which clearly indicates he has made another breakthrough and is even more advanced than Huayang; this too is a change.”

The Lord Emperor’s face showed contemplation.

It seemed as if the Longevity Pill was about to be completed; boundless cause and effect pressed down towards him from the invisible world, with changes unceasing and anomalies abounding.

This was also the case for Yu Hua who sought the Immortality Pill; nothing would go as she wished, and certainly not as the sect wished.

Wenren Wu exclaimed in surprise, “There’s still room for breakthrough at the peak of the Fourth Realm?”

“Not in terms of the realm, but closer to ‘Immortal.’ It is foreseeable that Huayang is inferior to Yun Miao; Yun Miao has achieved Dao Foundation Perfection at the Eighth Level, while Huayang is behind by one level, and between each level of Dao Foundation lies a whole sky; Perfection places one beyond the heavens, an insurmountable gap.”

The Lord Emperor glanced at the pill furnace, his usually serene eyes unusually fervent.

“I am at the same level as Yun Miao, but we both lack one level of Perfection; if I do not remedy this, I may never become an Immortal in this life.”

Wenren Wu’s face showed a bitter expression; he was only at Third Level Perfection, and his Dao Foundation was merely at the Eighth Level.

Achieving Dao Foundation is as difficult as ascending to the heavens, while Dao Foundation Perfection is like pushing a colossal boulder up the path to heaven.

He himself had been a military prodigy of his generation, and like Gu Wen, was capable of manifesting a dharma form; but in the end, he had stopped at the Eighth Level of Dao Foundation, achieving Perfection in just three of them.

The Lord Emperor took out a Golden Core, its spirit charm restrained, with the aura of the pill like a dragon.

“This pill can help you achieve Perfection in another level of your Dao Foundation, but this might be the last time you can take it; any more would be ineffective.”

Wenren Wu received the pill, unsure whether he was pleased or anxious.

To be stopped on the path to the Dao is utterly aggrieving!

At this moment, a guard hastily entered from outside the palace, bearing a document adorned with chicken feathers.

It’s known as a chicken feather document, which signifies urgency; hen feathers are attached to it to indicate it should be delivered swiftly.

The Lord Emperor opened it, glanced at it, and casually passed it to Wenren Wu, who twitched at the corner of his mouth after scanning it.

“Truly bold as brass; in such circumstances, they still have the mind to plunder official ships.”

Now the opposition was fully wanted by Daqian, with a bounty as high as ten thousand taels of silver.

For the various sects, an offer of a Taoist Soldier was promised, and some old monsters holding grudges against Qingcang would also come knocking.

Daqian was exerting its national power to hunt them down, with the Three Religions and myriad schools joining the pursuit.

Revealing his own location was to court death.

The Lord Emperor shook his head, “He is very shrewd, the safest place in the world is only when one has overwhelming power; until then, everything else is illusionary.

Hiding is to preserve life, rampaging through the world is to be invincible.”

“Then let us settle it in one fell swoop.” Wenren Wu, dragging his battered body, stood up, his aura filled with murderous intent, “Lead ten thousand elite soldiers to trample over, even if it shortens my lifespan, I must see him perish.”

The Lord Emperor nodded slightly, “Go, and when the time comes, I will help you hold off the Heavenly Girl for a moment.”

“As you command.”

Wenren Wu left the grand hall, and before stepping through the great doors, another messenger guard hastened into the imperial palace, bringing news, “Report!

Your Majesty, Zechuan County has fallen in battle, Minister of War Yuan Xiangchun has died in combat.”

The grand hall fell silent, the Lord Emperor sighed, “The affairs of the world are ever-changing, the secrets of heaven unpredictable, go and quell the rebellion.”

Wenren Wu, somewhat reluctantly said, “Gu Wen, this youngster, can refine his dharma form and Divine Skills amidst battle, he must not be left alive, Your Majesty.”

Methods of refining dharma form and Divine Skills are many and varied, learning to refine them amid battle is not unexpected, but Gu Wen learns too quickly.

“Zechuan unrest, and the whole world follows suit.”

The Lord Emperor knew the importance of the two; while Gu Wen may have a high talent, it is just that, talent.

No one could be sure of future achievements, but rebellion unquelled means the whole world will revolt.

One is a future threat, the other an axe poised to fall on one’s head.

“Understood.”

Wenren Wu bowed to receive the orders, then marched out of the imperial palace, took command of the military power outside of the imperial guard, and once again conscripted laborers.

Then there came another wave of wailing from Bianjing city, as countless male workers were dragged from their homes, some even captured by government officials right on the street.

Even large households weren’t spared; government officials came knocking to impose more taxes, and even scholar-official families could not escape.

Through pooling resources, an army of one hundred and fifty thousand was raised, the vast majority being laborers responsible for supply logistics.

The real force was an elite ten thousand returned from the frontier.

—————–

On the Qian River.

As soon as Gu Wen boarded, he was immediately spotted by the Grand Treasury Department’s guard, surrounded by a dozen knife-wielding government officials clad in chainmail, each looking robust, likely recruited from the imperial guard.

In ancient times, having armor made a significant difference.

These dozen or so men were enough to deter gangs of bandits consisting of hundreds, even thousands, from moving rashly.

Not every bandit was a hero of Liangshan, most were just starving vagrants with pitchforks; kill a dozen or so, and the rest would scatter.

After all, the Grand Treasury Department was tasked with collecting Spiritual Objects for the Emperor, so their personnel and equipment being excellent was understandable.

Otherwise, how to deal with being robbed?

Gu Wen condensed water into a spear and said, “This poor Daoist seeks only wealth, not lives.”

Now penniless, he was but a poor Daoist; with money, he would be a lord.

The surrounding government officials widened their eyes at this divine skill, then exchanged glances of bewilderment, and finally laid down their weapons.

A small-eyed eunuch emerged from a corner, clamoring, “Don’t be fooled by the tricks of this demonic Daoist.

These are tribute items required by the Saint Emperor; if they’re lost, you’ll all lose your heads!”

Bang!

The water spear flew out, piercing directly through the eunuch’s body and pinning him against the mast.

The eunuch’s eyes bulged wildly, his mouth spat fresh blood, and he screamed briefly before falling silent.

Silence!

Benevolent to others, Gu Wen said to the surrounding officials, “According to Daqian’s laws, resisting against overwhelming odds can be regarded as a meritorious deed.”

To fail to guard the court’s items meant beheading; if this rule were applied, nearly every official in charge of transport would meet death.

Given the inevitable losses in ancient transportation and the societal certainty of bandits in Daqian.

Even though Daqian was currently in turmoil, it was still considered enlightened and peaceful compared to other feudal dynasties, with neither cruel officials nor harsh laws.

Understanding his point, the officials dropped their weapons one after another, and then the leader stepped forward and asked, “What might the Immortal Master desire?”

“Medicinal tribute items.”

“Please follow me, Immortal Master.”

Gu Wen followed the man into the somewhat dim cabin, cramped and filled with goods.

Before he could stoop to inspect, a blade came swinging from behind him.

The blade’s icy gleam sought life, aiming a slash at the throat; a strike could easily sever a head from a flesh-and-blood body.

Gu Wen had no interest in testing the power of his protective Daoist skill; he turned and smashed a fist into one man’s skull, grabbed the sword and decapitated another.

The obstructing officials, seeing this, charged forward with fierce glints in their eyes, but none could withstand a single move from Gu Wen.

Heads rolled to the ground, tumbling side to side with the rocking of the ship.

Soon, all the officials aboard were dead.

A few jumped ship and fled; Gu Wen, not minding the trouble, disembarked to sink them one by one in the river.

Only three boatmen remained, who, upon seeing Gu Wen return, knelt and kowtowed for mercy.

It took a while to comfort them before the three boatmen could barely communicate and agreed to help find the tribute for him.

While the boatmen were moving goods, Gu Wen felt the Jade Pendant in his pocket repel his extended mana with a pop, which made him wince and say, “After exerting so much effort, it doesn’t serve this lord?”

Once out of danger, Gu Wen first thought of the Jade Pendant, rumored to contain a Taoist Soldier.

His Xuan Heavy Spear, hardly warmed by use before it broke, and Wenren Wu’s attacks had aimed mostly for it in hopes of capturing him alive.

And this Taoist Soldier was clearly not easy to refine; Gu Wen thought he needed to get some Emperor’s Jelly.

He had inquired about Emperor’s Jelly; his target was one of the tribute items from Heavenly Spring Water.

Originating from Luo River County, situated between South Water County and Qianjing County, and lying in Daqian’s central part, its handicrafts and commerce were extremely prosperous.

“Immortal Master, your items.”

The boatmen carried out box after box of goods and opened them one by one, containing silver, herbs, silk, and porcelain.

Gu Wen grabbed a handful of silver and tossed it to them, saying, “This is a reward for you, about a dozen taels each.

More, and you couldn’t carry it securely.”

The three boatmen hesitated.

Wouldn’t accepting it mean they were colluding?

The thought was fleeting.

Not everyone had the chance to collude, and they hadn’t been paid as government laborers!

One after another, without exception, they pocketed the silver.

Their fear of Gu Wen was washed away by the silver, and even a hint of admiration began to appear.

One of them plucked up the courage to ask, “May I know the benefactor’s name?”

“When did I become your benefactor?” Gu Wen said with a smile.

The boatman, young and strong, said respectfully, “The only male in my family, I was conscripted for forced labor and know not when I can return home.

Without the benefactor killing them, my elderly mother might have starved to death.”

“Here’s ten more taels for you.”

Amused, Gu Wen threw another ten taels and replied, “My surname is Gu, with a single name, Wen.

The old Emperor intended to pass the throne to me.

Today, I’m just collecting some interest.”

“…”

The boatman couldn’t contain himself.

He wanted to call Gu Wen a hero like those in the martial arts world, but Gu Wen spoke of becoming Emperor, and he didn’t know how to respond.

“Alright, dock the boat and get off.”

The boat neared the shore, and the three boatmen jumped out.

Gu Wen turned to search through the tribute items, unconcerned about a few innocent civilians escaping causing any trouble.

Reporting to the authorities risked being implicated, and considering the speed of information transmission in ancient times, the imperial soldiers would arrive long after he had fled.

This was why bandits existed in ancient times, yet now could hardly escape the province.

Rapidly enhancing one’s strength was fundamental, and the Fate Diagram could only be fulfilled by plundering.

A box of Spiritual Medicine, random and unrecognized herbs.

Gu Wen stuffed them into his mouth, holding a mandate token he had taken from the eunuch.

“Urgent dispatch over a thousand miles, and this place isn’t close to Zechuan?”

He read the message and was momentarily stunned.

“Lin Chuan County rebelled; the Prefectural Governor was killed by the rebels, and the army was defeated.”

Centered around Bianjing, Zechuan lay nearby, and beyond it was Lin Chuan.

There had been talk due to issues in Zechuan; only through South Water and Luo River counties could medicinal fruits from Lin Chuan come.

Meaning, this urgent dispatch from a remote area, sent over a thousand miles, was intercepted by him.

And Daqian remained oblivious, even as Lin Chuan had fallen.
